THE UNITED NATIONS ACT, No. 45 OF 1968 
Subsequent Amendments to the Consolidated List under Regulation 4(2)(b) of the 
United Nations Regulations No. 2 of 2012 
THE subsequent amendments, made on October 1, 2018 to the Consolidated List published in the Gazette  Extraordinary 
No. 1818/14 of June 11, 2013, of designated persons, referred to in Regulation 4(2)(b) of the United Nations Regulations 
No. 2 of 2012 published in the Gazette Extraordinary No. 1760/40 of May 31, 2012, shall be as specified in the Schedule 
hereto. 
General SHS Kottegoda (Retired) 
WWV RWP RSP VSV USP ndc 
Secretary,
Ministry of Defence, 
Competent Authority.Colombo, 
22nd May, 2019.
